After calling so many places most barbers would demand certain stuff after explaining what exactly my event was all about, but Not Jesus! Zay was very professional when he took my call and was kind to let me know he would return my call as soon as he would talk to his boss (Jesus). I was calling all the way from NorCal and trying to find someone to work for my event that took place in Palm Springs. It was a bit of a hassle but thank God I found diamond Cuts. Jesus and Jay took care of my needs and went above and beyond. I extremely recommend this barbershop ! Make sure to ask for Zay and Jesus for your next cut!

I will definitely be hiring them for my next event !</Review>

<userid>108148262281119792548< /userid>< review>
Being an African American visitor from the Columbus, Ohio area for a trip my wife won from her Company, Brookdale Senior Living, I was looking for a barber that would be able to take care of trimming and shaping my beard without worrying about whether it was the first time they would have done it for my hair type. After checking out the website, I decided to drive from the Hilton Miramonte Resort where we were staying to Cathedral City and Diamond Cuts for a walk-in.

I was given to Zay Aispuro, who not only was an engaging conversationalist, but a barber "par excellence". Where I was used to having clippers and scissors, Zay included hot towel treatment, straight razor edge and spray aftershave.

I not only highly recommend Zay, but the entire shop for anyone who is either visiting or lives in the Palm Springs area. It's worth the drive from wherever you are, because they will take excellent care of your needs. You will not be disappointed.<//review>

<UserId.>107521212673381242869<//UserId.><name>Craig Moen< /name><Date>1616963187694<//Date><rate>3< /rate>< review>
The employees at Dutch Brothers are always energetic, upbeat, and helpful. The coffee however is weak and in my opinion tasteless; and I always order a triple shot latte in a medium cup. I have never truly been satisfied with a Dutch Brothers latte which tastes mostly like sweet warm milk devoid of coffee flavor. The 3 stars are for Dutch Brothers fantastic staff and quick convenient drive through format. Please consider switching to more robust and flavorful coffee beans.Become a 5 star coffee leader.</review>

Update 1/20/21: After unpacking and sharing a document with all of the damaged and broken items from the move, Wes and the Qshark owner offered a significant sum to make things right by us and to cover some of the damages. --

Update: I've been working with Wes at QShark who has been very responsive in helping to resolve the situation. As we unpack we'll be in contact with them on the damages, and they will be refunding us a large portion of the initial cost.

---

I struggle to put into words how truly terrible our experience was. But I'll try‚Äîunprofessional, damaging and heartbreaking. I do not wish it upon any one. It took me just over two weeks to even write this review, because every time I think about it it makes me so upset.

*Here are the low lights*:

They advertise that they will come prepared with boxes to help you pack, and all you need to do is pay for the boxes you use. This is not true‚Äîthey do not come with boxes for purchase and they were clearly not interested in helping pack.

When they arrived and saw we still had some things which needed packing, they asked who was going to do it... I reminded them that that's why we hired them. They said "ok, all good. It's fine".

The only boxes they had come prepared with were MASSIVE (probably around 5 feet tall) wardrobe boxes. All we had left in the house to pack were things from the kitchen (glasses, plates, etc.) and other smaller items (ex: table lamps, audio equipment). Sometimes they placed our items in these massive boxes carefully, but often it felt like our stuff was just swimming inside the boxes, banging against one another.

I communicated to the lead mover, Robert, that we were going to be putting everything into storage in our new home since the house was not yet move in ready. So, I asked if we could keep things like the moving blankets on our designer furniture. He said I'd have to pay for them‚Äî$15 each. I said, no problem, I will pay for the blankets and the boxes.

As they were unpacking the belongings into the storage at our new house, we noticed they started unpacking the massive wardrobe boxes they had brought. We alerted them that since it's going into storage, to please not unpack them, and I restated I'd buy the boxes. Robert replied, "No, these are *my* boxes". Not only was everything clanking around inside during transport because they were too big, but they weren't available for me to buy as was advertised.

The same thing then also happened with our DWR furniture which I thought would be inside of the moving blankets. They unpacked them, and now there are scratches all over.

When unpacking, they cantilevered chairs on top of chairs next to delicate items. They placed a table on top of the couch, with stacks of boxes on top of it. All of our belongings precariously stored.

Since we weren't allowed to keep the boxes, many items are just sitting around, completely unpacked. We've already noticed some items are damaged, and I am scared to think what our fragile items and family heirlooms will be like... We bought a mattress cover for the mattress since it'd be inside in the construction area, and once I left, I realized they had removed the cover. So the mattress is now filthy from construction dust.

When they were done, he tried to get me to sign a customer satisfaction document. I felt extremely uncomfortable and pressured and intimidated by him to sign. I told him I was unhappy with the way things turned out, and he reminded me that they are professionals. I signed the first line, and then immediately crossed out my signature and wrote that I was unhappy and refused the sign the rest. He stormed out angrily.

*Positives*:
The crew under Robert were nice guys. They certainly intended well, but given the poor leadership, it was clear there was no quality bar they felt they needed to meet.< /text>

<review>We decided during quarantine, that this would be a great time to move. I went through Thumbtack and carefully read through tons of companies and reviews, and I stumbled across QShark. Their pricing was comparable to other companies, but the reviews were superior to all others. A week or so prior to our move date, I went ahead and booked with them. They confirmed everything over the phone and via email as well. The Called the night prior to our move go confirm everything. They didn't charge us any differently for a Sunday during memorial day weekend either, which really surprised me. The morning of, they called me an hour and a half prior to our start time, letting us know they'd be arriving at approximately 10:45am for our 11am time slot.

I met them downstairs as they wore masks for social distancing, Anthony and Eugene were our mover helpers! They filled out the start time as 10:55am and got to work right away.

They graciously worked with us and all of our things. I explained that since it was a short move(5 miles), I didn't need everything wrapped, just the dressers, fridge, tv stand and Rocking chair. They happily obliged. They worked at an even pace start to finish. They followed behind us at our new place, and due to spacing, they couldn't quite fit through the driveway. They made the trips back and forth getting all of our furniture in our new home.

I want to stop right here and say this: Never once did these guys complain about a single thing. They were the nicest, kindest people we could have asked for in this move. Moving can be stressful, but these guys took that all out of the equation.

Anyways, back to moving in. They were so quick to offer to jump in any time I maybe wanted to rearrange something because it fit a little better over there. They even took our couch apart and door off the hinge so our couch could fit in a certain room.

They out everything exactly where I asked them to. They treated myself and my husband with so much respect. These guys are honestly the only people I would allow to help me move again. They listened to me, heard what I asked, and did it joyfully. They're hard workers and I never saw them stop for anything.

Total cost: $428 for 4 Hours, 15 minutes for a Sunday rate of $89/hour and the $50 fuel fee.

As this was a long drive to our initial location, there was a $50 fuel fee but this was discussed prior to my booking their services.

I had NO last minute additional costs. They didn't add a single thing to our move or try to be sneaky at the end.

They're genuinely nice, hard working guys and I'd be happy to have them back next time, and to recommend them to anyone else moving.</review>< pics>
